have an existing system that generates X12 EDI files and you want to send them through Stedi.</p>
<ol>
<li>Call this endpoint with a payload in <a href="https://portal.stedi.com/app/guides/view/hipaa/health-care-claim-dental-x224a3/01GRYB6G91ZX6R1XAFGBMRTBBW" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">837 X12 EDI format</a>.</li>
<li>Stedi validates the EDI and sends the claim to the payer.</li>
<li>The endpoint returns a response from Stedi in JSON format containing information about the claim you submitted and whether the submission was successful.</li>

text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>A <code>200</code> response indicates that Stedi successfully generated the X12 EDI claim format required by the payer. It does not indicate whether the payer has accepted the claim - the payer will respond later with a 277CA containing this information. <a href="https://www.stedi.com/docs/healthcare/receive-claim-responses#response-types" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Learn more about 277CAs</a>. A <code>400</code> response indicates one or more problems with the claim data in the request. Examples include missing required fields, invalid values, or incorrect data types. The response includes a message describing the problem.</p><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>A <a href="https://www.stedi.com/docs/healthcare/claim-responses-overview#277ca-claim-acknowledgment" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">277CA claim acknowledgment</a> acceptance or rejection from Stedi in X12 EDI format. It indicates whether the claim has passed Stedi&#x27;s claim edits.</p>
<p>When the claim fails one or more edits, the 277CA contains <code>STC</code> segments with information about each error. These are the same error codes that appear in the <code>errors</code> array.</p>
<p>Note that this 277CA only indicates whether Stedi has accepted or rejected the claim submission. You may receive additional 277CA acceptances or rejections as the claim is routed to the payer.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="hidden xl:flex xl:flex-col self-start sticky gap-6 max-w-[28rem] h-[calc(100vh-11rem)] top-[10rem]"><div class="w-full xl:w-[28rem] grid grid-rows-[repeat(auto-fit,minmax(0,min-content))] relative max-h-[calc(100%-32px)] min-h-[18rem]
